Class otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::derivAffirm extends model::domain::transactional::trading::contract::event::transmission::DerivAffirm, otcConsumerModel::model::objectMetadata
{
  relatedDealEvent: otcConsumerModel::model::tradeProcessing::dealEvent[1];
  derivConfirmAssetClass() {if(
  $this.domain->in(
    [
      'SNOWDON',
      'KASAI',
      'CONGO',
      'ELBRUS',
      'UBANGI',
      'SANGHA'
    ]
  ),
  |'EQ',
  |if(

function otcConsumerModel::function::valuation::bcxLatestNetMonetaryMeasure(bcxNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasures: otcConsumerModel::model::valuation::bcxNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasure[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $bcxNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasures->filter(
    x|((($x.valuationDate >
      $businessDate->meta::pure::functions::date::adjust(
      meta::pure::functions::math::minus(2),
      meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.YEARS
    )) &&
      ($x.valuationDate <=
      $businessDate)) &&
      (($x.currency != 'NA') &&
      ($x.lake_out_id == 999999999))) &&
      (($x.holdableType == 'CONTRACT') &&
      $x.valuationScenario->in(
      [
        'CSA',
        'OIS',
        'LBR'
      ]
    ))
  )->groupBy(
    [
      x|$x.holdableId,
      x|$x.valuationDate,
      x|$x.valuationScenario,
      x|$x.valuationScenarioRanking,
      x|$x.valuationType,
      x|$x.valuationTypeRanking,
      x|$x.currency,
      x|$x.groupType,
      x|$x.groupTypeRanking
    ],
    [
      agg(
        x|$x.amountInUsd,
        x|$x->sum()->abs()
      )
    ],
    [
      'HoldableId',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'ValuationScenarioRanking',
      'ValuationType',
      'ValuationTypeRanking',
      'Currency',
      'GroupType',
      'GroupTypeRanking',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    desc('ValuationDate'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxValuationDateIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxValuationDateIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    asc('ValuationScenarioRanking'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxValuationScenarioIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxValuationScenarioIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    asc('ValuationTypeRanking'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxValuationTypeIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxValuationTypeIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    asc('GroupTypeRanking'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxGroupTypeIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxGroupTypeIndex') == 1
  )->restrict(
    [
      'HoldableId',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'ValuationType',
      'Currency',
      'GroupType',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )
}

{

      ]

      ($x.timeUpdated->datePart() <=
      $businessDate)

      'ConfirmTechVersion',
      'Source',

      'DateUpdated',
      'ConfirmPlatform',
      'RenderingChannel',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    'DateUpdated'->func(
      x|$x->min()
    ),
    'DerivConfirmCreationDate'
  )->join(
    $refinedDerivativeConfirms->otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unsignedLegalConfirms::refinedDerivativeConfirmDeemedAcceptance(),

  )->join(

    ['RelatedContractEventId_FXVanillaTrade']
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'TimeUpdated'
    ],

    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'techVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('techVersionIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    desc('TimeUpdated'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'timeUpdatedIndex'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    desc('ConfirmVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'confirmVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|(($row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('confirmVersionIndex') == 1)) ||
      (!$row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('timeUpdatedIndex') == 1))) &&
      !$row.getString('Status')->in(
      [
        'AWAITING_SUPPRESSION_APPROVAL',
        'CONFIRMED',
        'NOT_REQUIRED',
        'TRANSMITTED',
        'GENERATED',
        'GROUP_SUPPRESSED',
        'GROUP_TRANSMITTED',

        'NOT_REQUIRED_PENDING_RESPONSE',
        'CHASER_EXPIRED',
        'CHASER_GROUPED'
      ]
    )
  )->extend(

    ]
  )->join(

      x|!(($x.secDbTradeableClassification == 'CT Funding Fixed') ||
        ($x.secDbTradeableClassification == 'CT Funding Float')) &&
        ($x.eventDate <=
        $businessDate)
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.traderBookingLocation,
        x|$x.eventDate,
        x|if(

        |$x.riskAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel3.name
      ),
        x|if(

        'ContractEventStatus',
        'ContractId',
        'DaysSinceEventDate'
      ]
    )->distinct(),

      'RelatedContractEventId',
      'RelatedContractEventVersion'
    ],
    [
      'ContractEventId',
      'ContractEventVersion'
    ]
  )->filter(
    row|!(($row.getString('Source') == 'DXP') &&
      ($row.getString('PrimaryAssetClass') == 'Equity'))
  )->filter(
    row|($row.getString('PrimaryAssetClass') == 'Equity') ||
      (($row.getString('PrimaryAssetClass') != 'Equity') &&
      ($row.getString('DeemedAcceptance') != 'YES'))
  )->filter(

function otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unsignedLegalConfirms::refinedDerivativeConfirmDeemedAcceptance(refinedDerivativeConfirms: otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm[*]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedDerivativeConfirms->filter(
    x|(($x.confirmType == 'IncomingConfirm') &&
      ($x.reason == 'DEEMED_ACCEPTANCE')) &&
      ($x.confirmRole == 'LEGAL')
  )->groupBy(
    [
      x|$x.contractEventId,
      x|'YES'
    ],
    [
      agg(
        x|$x.contractEventId,
        x|$x->count()
      )
    ],
    [
      'RelatedContractEventId_DeemedAcceptance',
      'DeemedAcceptance',
      'count_deemedAcceptance'
    ]
  )
}

function {otcConsumerModel::profile::gsMetricsProfile.metricId = '68232c9978d54160c9e17990', otcConsumerModel::profile::gsMetricsProfile.metricId = '6825e1c0bc8fa95c326c2b96', otcConsumerModel::profile::gsMetricsProfile.metricId = '6825e0c0b64eaf5f0b2664be'} otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::refinedPayment_FailedSettlements(refinedPayment: otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedPayment[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedPayment->filter(
    x|($x.creationTimeStamp->datePart() <=
      $businessDate) &&
      $x.parentPaymentId->isEmpty()
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.cashflowNetId,
      x|$x.cashflowNetVersion,
      x|$x.techVersion,
      x|$x.domain,
      x|$x.status,
      x|$x.paymentDate,
      x|$x.parentPaymentId,
      x|$x.parentPaymentVersion,
      x|$x.amount,
      x|if(
      $x.amount < 0,
      |'Pay',
      |'Receive'
    ),
      x|$x.currency,
      x|$x.amountInUsd($businessDate, model::domain::referenceData::price::fx::FundingScenarioEnum.FEDFUND, model::domain::referenceData::geography::BusinessCenter.USNY),
      x|$x.settlementInstruction,
      x|$x.paymentShape,
      x|$x.responsibility,
      x|$x.annotation,
      x|$x.creationTimeStamp,
      x|$x.creationUserId,
      x|$x.age,
      x|$x.earliestPaymentDate
    ],
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'CashflowNetIdPayment',
      'CashflowNetVersionPayment',
      'TechVersion',
      'Domain',
      'PaymentStatusParent',
      'PaymentDate',
      'ParentPaymentId',
      'ParentPaymentVersion',
      'PaymentAmount',
      'PaymentDirection',
      'PaymentCurrency',
      'PaymentAmountUSD',
      'SettlementInstruction',
      'PaymentShape',
      'Responsibility',
      'Annotation',
      'CreationTimeStamp',
      'CreationUserId',
      'Age',
      'EarliestPaymentDate'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'Domain'
    ],
    'PaymentVersion'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'max of Payment Version'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'Domain'
    ],
    'TechVersion'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'max of Tech version'
  )->filter(
    row|((($row.getStrictDate('EarliestPaymentDate') <=
      $businessDate) &&
      (($row.getInteger('PaymentVersion') ==
      $row.getNumber('max of Payment Version')) &&
      ($row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
      $row.getNumber('max of Tech version')))) &&
      ($row.getString('Responsibility') != 'Term Deposit Team')) &&
      ($row.getString('Responsibility') != 'KOR IRP Team')
  )->restrict(
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'CashflowNetIdPayment',
      'CashflowNetVersionPayment',
      'Domain',
      'PaymentStatusParent',
      'PaymentDate',
      'EarliestPaymentDate',
      'ParentPaymentId',
      'ParentPaymentVersion',
      'PaymentAmount',
      'PaymentDirection',
      'PaymentCurrency',
      'PaymentAmountUSD',
      'SettlementInstruction',
      'PaymentShape',
      'Responsibility',
      'Annotation',
      'CreationTimeStamp',
      'CreationUserId',
      'Age'
    ]
  )->join(
    $refinedPayment->otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::getPartialPayments(
      $businessDate
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'Domain'
    ],
    [
      'ParentPaymentIdChild',
      'DomainChild'
    ]
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          !$r.getString('ParentPaymentIdChild')->isEmpty() &&
            $r.getString('PaymentStatusParent')->in(
            [
              'Cancelled',
              'NotRequired',
              'Banked',
              'SuppressedWithJournals',
              'Ceased',
              'WrittenOff',
              'Suppressed'
            ]
          ),
          |'Partial Settle',
          |$r.getString('PaymentStatusParent')
        ),
        'PaymentStatus'
      )
    ]
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          !$r.getString('ParentPaymentIdChild')->isEmpty(),
          |$r.getString('PaymentStatusParent'),
          |''
        ),
        'ParentPaymentStatus'
      )
    ]
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          $r.getString('PaymentStatus') == 'Partial Settle',
          |$r.getFloat('ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD'),
          |if(
            $r.getFloat('ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD')->isEmpty(),
            |0,
            |$r.getFloat('ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD')
          ) + $r.getFloat('PaymentAmountUSD')
        ),
        'TotalPendingAmountUSD'
      )
    ]
  )->filter(
    row|!$row.getString('PaymentStatus')->in(
      [
        'Cancelled',
        'NotRequired',
        'Banked',
        'SuppressedWithJournals',
        'Ceased',
        'WrittenOff',
        'Suppressed'
      ]
    )
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedCashflowNet.all()->filter(
      x|$x.creationTimeStamp->datePart() <=
        $businessDate
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.techVersion,
        x|$x.domain,
        x|$x.settlementGsParty,
        x|$x.settlementCounterParty,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).beneficialOwnerEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).investmentAdvisorEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.facetClientDetails($businessDate, $businessDate).reportingEntity.divisionalReportingGroup.name,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).accountCategorization.intercompanyAccount,
        x|$x.legacyNetTypeId
      ],
      [
        'CashflowNetId',
        'CashflowNetVersion',
        'TechVersion',
        'DomainCashflowNet',
        'SettlementGsParty',
        'SettlementCounterParty',
        'BenificialOwnerLegalName',
        'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
        'IntercompanyIndicator',
        'LegacyNetTypeId'
      ]
    )->distinct()->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'CashflowNetId',
        'DomainCashflowNet',
        'CashflowNetVersion'
      ],
      'TechVersion'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Tech Version'
    )->filter(
      row|($row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Tech Version')) &&
        !(($row.getString('LegacyNetTypeId') == 'SPGXProd_PB') ||
        ($row.getString('LegacyNetTypeId') == 'SPGXProd_Synthetic'))
    )->restrict(
      [
        'CashflowNetId',
        'CashflowNetVersion',
        'DomainCashflowNet',
        'SettlementGsParty',
        'SettlementCounterParty',
        'BenificialOwnerLegalName',
        'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
        'IntercompanyIndicator',
        'LegacyNetTypeId'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.INNER,
    [
      'CashflowNetIdPayment',
      'CashflowNetVersionPayment',
      'Domain'
    ],
    [
      'CashflowNetId',
      'CashflowNetVersion',
      'DomainCashflowNet'
    ]
  )->restrict(
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'CashflowNetId',
      'CashflowNetVersion',
      'Domain',
      'PaymentStatus',
      'ParentPaymentStatus',
      'PaymentDate',
      'EarliestPaymentDate',
      'PaymentAmount',
      'PaymentDirection',
      'PaymentCurrency',
      'PaymentAmountUSD',
      'ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD',
      'TotalPendingAmountUSD',
      'SettlementInstruction',
      'PaymentShape',
      'Responsibility',
      'Annotation',
      'CreationTimeStamp',
      'CreationUserId',
      'Age',
      'SettlementGsParty',
      'SettlementCounterParty',
      'BenificialOwnerLegalName',
      'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
      'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
      'IntercompanyIndicator',
      'LegacyNetTypeId'
    ]
  )
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unsentLegalConfirms::getUnsentGCONContractEventIDs(refinedDerivativeConfirms: otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedDerivativeConfirms->filter(
    x|((($x.confirmType == 'GroupedOutgoingConfirm') &&
      ((($x.confirmRole == 'LEGAL') &&
      ($x.source != 'CCT')) &&
      ($x.sourceSystem != 'CCT'))) &&
      $x.domain->in(
      [
        'SNOWDON',
        'DOM',
        'KASAI',
        'CONGO',
        'ELBRUS',
        'UBANGI',
        'SANGHA',
        'NILE',
        'MCKINLEY',
        'GANGES',
        'INDUS',
        'SUTLEJ',
        'RHINE',
        'VOLGA',
        'SANFORD',
        'YANGTZE',
        'DANUBE'
      ]
    )) &&
      ($x.timeUpdated->datePart() <=
      $businessDate)
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.status,
      x|$x.reason,
      x|$x.comments,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.techVersion,
      x|$x.timeUpdated,
      x|$x.timeUpdated->datePart(),
      x|$x.domain,
      x|$x.derivConfirmAssetClass,
      x|$x.objectId->substring(
      0,
      $x.objectId->indexOf('-') - 1
    )
    ],
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'GroupStatus',
      'GroupReason',
      'GroupComments',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'ConfirmTechVersion',
      'TimeUpdated',
      'DateUpdated',
      'Domain_GCON',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass_GCON',
      'AssociatedGroupId_GCON'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    'DateUpdated'->func(
      x|$x->min()
    ),
    'DerivConfirmCreationDate'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'TimeUpdated',
      'Domain_GCON'
    ],
    desc('ConfirmTechVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'techVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('techVersionIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'Domain_GCON'
    ],
    desc('TimeUpdated'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'timeUpdatedIndex'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'Domain_GCON'
    ],
    desc('ConfirmVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'confirmVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|(($row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('confirmVersionIndex') == 1)) ||
      (!$row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('timeUpdatedIndex') ==
      1 == 1))) &&
      ($row.getString('GroupStatus') == 'AWAITING_APPROVAL')
  )->restrict(
    [
      'GroupStatus',
      'GroupReason',
      'GroupComments',
      'Domain_GCON',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass_GCON',
      'AssociatedGroupId_GCON',
      'DerivConfirmCreationDate'
    ]
  )->distinct()->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm.all()->filter(
      x|((($x.confirmType == 'OutgoingConfirm') &&
        ((($x.confirmRole == 'LEGAL') &&
        ($x.source != 'CCT')) &&
        ($x.sourceSystem != 'CCT'))) &&
        $x.domain->in(
        [
          'SNOWDON',
          'DOM',
          'KASAI',
          'CONGO',
          'ELBRUS',
          'UBANGI',
          'SANGHA',
          'NILE',
          'MCKINLEY',
          'GANGES',
          'INDUS',
          'SUTLEJ',
          'RHINE',
          'VOLGA',
          'SANFORD',
          'YANGTZE',
          'DANUBE'
        ]
      )) &&
        ($x.timeUpdated->datePart() <=
        $businessDate)
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.domain,
        x|$x.contractEventId,
        x|$x.contractEventVersion,
        x|$x.status,
        x|$x.reason,
        x|$x.comments,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.techVersion,
        x|$x.source,
        x|$x.timeUpdated,
        x|$x.associatedGroupId,
        x|$x.confirmPlatform,
        x|$x.renderingChannel,
        x|$x.derivConfirmAssetClass
      ],
      [
        'ConfirmId',
        'Domain',
        'RelatedContractEventId',
        'RelatedContractEventVersion',
        'Status',
        'Reason',
        'Comments',
        'ConfirmVersion',
        'ConfirmTechVersion',
        'Source',
        'TimeUpdated',
        'AssociatedGroupID',
        'ConfirmPlatform',
        'RenderingChannel',
        'DerivConfirmAssetClass'
      ]
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'ConfirmId',
        'ConfirmVersion',
        'TimeUpdated'
      ],
      desc('ConfirmTechVersion'),
      x|$x->rowNumber(),
      'techVersionIndex'
    )->filter(
      row|$row.getNumber('techVersionIndex') == 1
    )->olapGroupBy(
      ['ConfirmId'],
      desc('TimeUpdated'),
      x|$x->rowNumber(),
      'timeUpdatedIndex'
    )->olapGroupBy(
      ['ConfirmId'],
      desc('ConfirmVersion'),
      x|$x->rowNumber(),
      'confirmVersionIndex'
    )->filter(
      row|((($row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
        ($row.getNumber('confirmVersionIndex') == 1)) ||
        (!$row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
        ($row.getNumber('timeUpdatedIndex') ==
        1 == 1))) &&
        !$row.getString('AssociatedGroupID')->isEmpty()) &&
        !$row.getString('Status')->in(
        [
          'AWAITING_SUPPRESSION_APPROVAL',
          'CONFIRMED',
          'NOT_REQUIRED',
          'TRANSMITTED',
          'GROUP_SUPPRESSED',
          'GROUP_TRANSMITTED',
          'CHASER_TRANSMITTED',
          'CHASER_SNOOZED',
          'NOT_REQUIRED_PENDING_RESPONSE',
          'CHASER_EXPIRED',
          'CHASER_GROUPED'
        ]
      )
    )->restrict(
      [
        'ConfirmId',
        'Domain',
        'RelatedContractEventId',
        'RelatedContractEventVersion',
        'Status',
        'Reason',
        'Comments',
        'TimeUpdated',
        'ConfirmVersion',
        'ConfirmTechVersion',
        'Source',
        'AssociatedGroupID',
        'ConfirmPlatform',
        'RenderingChannel',
        'DerivConfirmAssetClass'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.INNER,
    [
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass_GCON',
      'AssociatedGroupId_GCON'
    ],
    [
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'AssociatedGroupID'
    ]
  )->restrict(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'RelatedContractEventId',
      'RelatedContractEventVersion',
      'Status',
      'Reason',
      'Comments',
      'TimeUpdated',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'ConfirmTechVersion',
      'Source',
      'AssociatedGroupID',
      'ConfirmPlatform',
      'RenderingChannel',
      'GroupStatus',
      'GroupReason',
      'GroupComments',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'DerivConfirmCreationDate'
    ]
  )
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::union_CashflowObjects(refinedCashflow: otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedCashflow[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedCashflow->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.domain,
      x|$x.techVersion,
      x|$x.currency,
      x|$x.amount,
      x|$x.paymentDate,
      x|$x.party1,
      x|$x.party2,
      x|$x.status,
      x|$x.cashflowType,
      x|'',
      x|$x.source,
      x|$x.contractEventId,
      x|$x.contractEventVersion,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel1.name,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel2.name,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel3.name,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel4.name,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel5.name,
      x|$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel6.name,
      x|$x.xstoreCreationTimeStamp
    ],
    [
      'CashflowId',
      'CashflowVersion',
      'DomainCashflow',
      'TechVersion',
      'Currency',
      'Amount',
      'CashflowPaymentDate',
      'CashflowParty1',
      'CashflowParty2',
      'CashflowStatus',
      'CashflowType',
      'SyntheticType',
      'Source',
      'ContractEventIdCashflow',
      'ContractEventVersionCashflow',
      'SbhLevel1',
      'SbhLevel2',
      'SbhLevel3',
      'SbhLevel4',
      'SbhLevel5',
      'SbhLevel6',
      'CashflowXstoreCreationTimestamp'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'CashflowId',
      'CashflowVersion',
      'DomainCashflow'
    ],
    'TechVersion'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'max of Tech version'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
      $row.getNumber('max of Tech version')
  )->restrict(
    [
      'CashflowId',
      'CashflowVersion',
      'DomainCashflow',
      'Currency',
      'Amount',
      'CashflowPaymentDate',
      'CashflowParty1',
      'CashflowParty2',
      'CashflowStatus',
      'CashflowType',
      'SyntheticType',
      'Source',
      'ContractEventIdCashflow',
      'ContractEventVersionCashflow',
      'SbhLevel1',
      'SbhLevel2',
      'SbhLevel3',
      'SbhLevel4',
      'SbhLevel5',
      'SbhLevel6'
    ]
  )->concatenate(
    otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedSyntheticCashflow.all()->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.techVersion,
        x|$x.domain,
        x|$x.currency,
        x|$x.amount,
        x|$x.paymentDate,
        x|$x.party1,
        x|$x.party2,
        x|$x.status,
        x|$x.cashflowType,
        x|$x.syntheticType,
        x|$x.source,
        x|'',
        x|-1,
        x|'',
        x|'',
        x|'',
        x|'',
        x|'',
        x|'',
        x|$x.xstoreCreationTimeStamp
      ],
      [
        'CashflowId',
        'CashflowVersion',
        'TechVersion',
        'DomainCashflow',
        'Currency',
        'Amount',
        'CashflowPaymentDate',
        'CashflowParty1',
        'CashflowParty2',
        'CashflowStatus',
        'CashflowType',
        'SyntheticType',
        'Source',
        'ContractEventIdCashflow',
        'ContractEventVersionCashflow',
        'SbhLevel1',
        'SbhLevel2',
        'SbhLevel3',
        'SbhLevel4',
        'SbhLevel5',
        'SbhLevel6',
        'CashflowXstoreCreationTimestamp'
      ]
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'CashflowId',
        'CashflowVersion',
        'DomainCashflow'
      ],
      'TechVersion'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Tech version'
    )->filter(
      row|$row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Tech version')
    )->restrict(
      [
        'CashflowId',
        'CashflowVersion',
        'DomainCashflow',
        'Currency',
        'Amount',
        'CashflowPaymentDate',
        'CashflowParty1',
        'CashflowParty2',
        'CashflowStatus',
        'CashflowType',
        'SyntheticType',
        'Source',
        'ContractEventIdCashflow',
        'ContractEventVersionCashflow',
        'SbhLevel1',
        'SbhLevel2',
        'SbhLevel3',
        'SbhLevel4',
        'SbhLevel5',
        'SbhLevel6'
      ]
    )
  )
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::getPartialPayments(refinedPayment: otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedPayment[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedPayment->filter(
    x|($x.creationTimeStamp->datePart() <=
      $businessDate) &&
      !$x.parentPaymentId->isEmpty()
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.techVersion,
      x|$x.domain,
      x|$x.status,
      x|$x.parentPaymentId,
      x|$x.parentPaymentVersion,
      x|$x.paymentDate,
      x|$x.amount,
      x|$x.amountInUsd($businessDate, model::domain::referenceData::price::fx::FundingScenarioEnum.FEDFUND, model::domain::referenceData::geography::BusinessCenter.USNY)
    ],
    [
      'PaymentIdChild',
      'PaymentVersionChild',
      'TechVersionChild',
      'DomainChild',
      'PaymentStatusChild',
      'ParentPaymentIdChild',
      'ParentPaymentVersionChild',
      'PaymentDateChild',
      'PaymentAmountChild',
      'PaymentAmountChildUSD'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'PaymentIdChild',
      'DomainChild'
    ],
    'PaymentVersionChild'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'max of Payment Version'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'PaymentIdChild',
      'PaymentVersionChild',
      'DomainChild'
    ],
    'TechVersionChild'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'max of Tech version'
  )->filter(
    row|!$row.getString('PaymentStatusChild')->in(
      [
        'Cancelled',
        'NotRequired',
        'Banked',
        'SuppressedWithJournals',
        'Ceased',
        'WrittenOff',
        'Suppressed'
      ]
    ) &&
      (($row.getStrictDate('PaymentDateChild') <=
      $businessDate) &&
      (($row.getInteger('PaymentVersionChild') ==
      $row.getNumber('max of Payment Version')) &&
      ($row.getInteger('TechVersionChild') ==
      $row.getNumber('max of Tech version'))))
  )->groupBy(
    [
      'DomainChild',
      'ParentPaymentIdChild'
    ],
    [
      'ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD'->agg(
      r|$r.getFloat('PaymentAmountChildUSD'),
      c|$c->sum()
    )
    ]
  )->restrict(
    [
      'ParentPaymentIdChild',
      'DomainChild',
      'ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD'
    ]
  )->distinct()
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::refinedPayableCashflow_FailedSettlements(payment: otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedPayment[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $payment->otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::refinedPayment_FailedSettlements(
    $businessDate
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedPaymentPayableCashflowMapping.all()->filter(
      x|$x.paymentCreationTimeStamp->datePart() <=
        $businessDate
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.domain,
        x|$x.paymentId,
        x|$x.paymentVersion,
        x|$x.payableCashflowId,
        x|$x.payableCashflowVersion,
        x|$x.tech_version,
        x|$x.paymentDate
      ],
      [
        'DomainPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentIdPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PayableCashflowIdPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PayableCashflowVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
        'TechVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentDatePaymentPayableMapping'
      ]
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'DomainPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentIdPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping'
      ],
      'TechVersionPaymentPayableMapping'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Tech version'
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'DomainPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentIdPaymentPayableMapping'
      ],
      'PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Payment version'
    )->filter(
      row|($row.getInteger('TechVersionPaymentPayableMapping') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Tech version')) &&
        ($row.getInteger('PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Payment version'))
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'DomainPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentIdPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
        'PayableCashflowIdPaymentPayableMapping',
        'TechVersionPaymentPayableMapping'
      ],
      'PayableCashflowVersionPaymentPayableMapping'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Payable Cashflow version'
    )->filter(
      row|$row.getInteger('PayableCashflowVersionPaymentPayableMapping') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Payable Cashflow version')
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.INNER,
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'Domain'
    ],
    [
      'PaymentIdPaymentPayableMapping',
      'PaymentVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
      'DomainPaymentPayableMapping'
    ]
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedPayableCashflow.all()->filter(
      x|$x.creationTimeStamp->datePart() <=
        $businessDate
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.domain,
        x|$x.techVersion,
        x|$x.cashflowId,
        x|$x.cashflowVersion,
        x|$x.cashflowNetId,
        x|$x.cashflowNetVersion,
        x|$x.amount,
        x|$x.currency,
        x|$x.amountInUsd($businessDate, model::domain::referenceData::price::fx::FundingScenarioEnum.FEDFUND, model::domain::referenceData::geography::BusinessCenter.USNY),
        x|$x.paymentDate,
        x|$x.settlementGsParty,
        x|$x.settlementCounterParty,
        x|$x.status,
        x|$x.dealId,
        x|$x.xstoreCreationTimeStamp,
        x|$x.partitionCol,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).beneficialOwnerEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).investmentAdvisorEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.facetClientDetails($businessDate, $businessDate).reportingEntity.divisionalReportingGroup.name,
        x|$x.creationTimeStamp
      ],
      [
        'PayableCashflowId',
        'PayableCashflowVersion',
        'DomainPayableCashflow',
        'TechVersion',
        'CashflowIdPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowVersionPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowNetIdPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowNetVersionPayableCashflow',
        'PayableCashflowAmount',
        'PayableCashflowCurrency',
        'PayableCashflowAmountUSD',
        'PayableCashflowPaymentDate',
        'PayableCashflowParty1',
        'PayableCashflowParty2',
        'PayableCashflowStatus',
        'XstoreGroupId',
        'XstoreCreationTimeStamp',
        'PartitionCol',
        'PayableCashflowBenificialOwnerLegalName',
        'PayableCashflowInvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'PayableCashflowFacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
        'PayableCashflowCreationTimeStamp'
      ]
    )->olapGroupBy(
      [
        'PayableCashflowId',
        'PayableCashflowVersion',
        'DomainPayableCashflow'
      ],
      'TechVersion'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'max of Tech version'
    )->filter(
      row|$row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
        $row.getNumber('max of Tech version')
    )->restrict(
      [
        'PayableCashflowId',
        'PayableCashflowVersion',
        'DomainPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowIdPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowVersionPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowNetIdPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowNetVersionPayableCashflow',
        'PayableCashflowAmount',
        'PayableCashflowCurrency',
        'PayableCashflowAmountUSD',
        'PayableCashflowPaymentDate',
        'PayableCashflowParty1',
        'PayableCashflowParty2',
        'PayableCashflowStatus',
        'XstoreGroupId',
        'XstoreCreationTimeStamp',
        'PartitionCol',
        'PayableCashflowBenificialOwnerLegalName',
        'PayableCashflowInvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'PayableCashflowFacetDivisionalReportingGroupName'
      ]
    )->join(
      otcConsumerModel::model::settlement::refinedCashflow.all()->otcConsumerModel::function::settlement::union_CashflowObjects(
        $businessDate
      ),
      meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
      [
        'CashflowIdPayableCashflow',
        'CashflowVersionPayableCashflow'
      ],
      [
        'CashflowId',
        'CashflowVersion'
      ]
    )->join(
      otcConsumerModel::model::tradeProcessing::refinedContractEvent.all()->project(
        [
          x|$x.objectId,
          x|$x.domain,
          x|$x.version,
          x|$x.techVersion,
          x|$x.gsDirection,
          x|$x.externalTradeId,
          x|$x.secDbTradeableClassification,
          x|$x.primaryAssetClass,
          x|$x.counterParty1Account,
          x|$x.counterParty2Account,
          x|$x.tradeType,
          x|$x.traderBookingLocation,
          x|$x.traderKerberos,
          x|$x.contractEventStatus
        ],
        [
          'ContractEventId',
          'DomainContractEvent',
          'ContractEventVersion',
          'TechVersion',
          'GsDirection',
          'ExternalTradeId',
          'SecDbTradeableClassification',
          'PrimaryAssetClass',
          'CounterParty1Account',
          'CounterParty2Account',
          'TradeType',
          'TraderBookingLocation',
          'TraderKerberos',
          'ContractEventStatus'
        ]
      )->olapGroupBy(
        [
          'ContractEventId',
          'ContractEventVersion'
        ],
        'TechVersion'->func(
          x|$x->max()
        ),
        'max of Tech Version'
      )->filter(
        row|$row.getInteger('TechVersion') ==
          $row.getNumber('max of Tech Version')
      )->restrict(
        [
          'ContractEventId',
          'ContractEventVersion',
          'DomainContractEvent',
          'GsDirection',
          'ExternalTradeId',
          'SecDbTradeableClassification',
          'PrimaryAssetClass',
          'CounterParty1Account',
          'CounterParty2Account',
          'TradeType',
          'TraderBookingLocation',
          'TraderKerberos',
          'ContractEventStatus'
        ]
      ),
      meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
      [
        'ContractEventIdCashflow',
        'ContractEventVersionCashflow',
        'DomainCashflow'
      ],
      [
        'ContractEventId',
        'ContractEventVersion',
        'DomainContractEvent'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    [
      'PayableCashflowIdPaymentPayableMapping',
      'PayableCashflowVersionPaymentPayableMapping',
      'Domain'
    ],
    [
      'PayableCashflowId',
      'PayableCashflowVersion',
      'DomainPayableCashflow'
    ]
  )->filter(
    row|($row.getString('PayableCashflowStatus') != 'Cancelled') &&
      ($row.getDate('PayableCashflowPaymentDate') <=
      $businessDate)
  )->filter(
    row|(($row.getString('CashflowType') == 'TAX') ||
      $row.getString('CashflowType')->isEmpty()) ||
      (($row.getString('SyntheticType') == 'CreditClsCashflow') ||
      ($row.getString('SyntheticType') == ''))
  )->restrict(
    [
      'PaymentId',
      'PaymentVersion',
      'CashflowNetId',
      'CashflowNetVersion',
      'Domain',
      'PaymentStatus',
      'ParentPaymentStatus',
      'PaymentDate',
      'EarliestPaymentDate',
      'PaymentAmount',
      'PaymentDirection',
      'PaymentCurrency',
      'PaymentAmountUSD',
      'ChildPendingPaymentAmountUSD',
      'TotalPendingAmountUSD',
      'SettlementInstruction',
      'PaymentShape',
      'Responsibility',
      'Annotation',
      'CreationTimeStamp',
      'CreationUserId',
      'Age',
      'SettlementGsParty',
      'SettlementCounterParty',
      'BenificialOwnerLegalName',
      'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
      'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
      'IntercompanyIndicator',
      'LegacyNetTypeId',
      'PayableCashflowId',
      'PayableCashflowVersion',
      'PayableCashflowAmount',
      'PayableCashflowCurrency',
      'PayableCashflowAmountUSD',
      'PayableCashflowPaymentDate',
      'PayableCashflowParty1',
      'PayableCashflowParty2',
      'PayableCashflowStatus',
      'PayableCashflowBenificialOwnerLegalName',
      'PayableCashflowInvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
      'PayableCashflowFacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
      'CashflowId',
      'CashflowVersion',
      'Currency',
      'Amount',
      'CashflowPaymentDate',
      'CashflowParty1',
      'CashflowParty2',
      'CashflowStatus',
      'CashflowType',
      'SyntheticType',
      'Source',
      'SbhLevel1',
      'SbhLevel2',
      'SbhLevel3',
      'SbhLevel4',
      'SbhLevel5',
      'SbhLevel6',
      'ContractEventId',
      'ContractEventVersion',
      'DomainContractEvent',
      'GsDirection',
      'ExternalTradeId',
      'SecDbTradeableClassification',
      'PrimaryAssetClass',
      'CounterParty1Account',
      'CounterParty2Account',
      'TradeType',
      'TraderBookingLocation',
      'TraderKerberos',
      'ContractEventStatus'
    ]
  )
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unaffirmedFinancialConfirms::directUnaffirmedFinancialConfirms(directDerivativeAffirms: otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::derivAffirm[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $directDerivativeAffirms->filter(
    x|$x.lakePartition >= 19723
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.ts->datePart(),
      x|$x.dealId,
      x|$x.derivConfirmAssetClass,
      x|$x.venue.platform->toOne()->toString(),
      x|'N/A',
      x|$x.confirmable.state.status->toOne()->toString(),
      x|$x.confirmable.state.reason
    ],
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'DerivAffirmVersion',
      'DerivAffirmTimestampDate',
      'ContractId',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'ConfirmPlatform',
      'RenderingChannel',
      'Status',
      'Reason'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    'DerivAffirmVersion'->func(
      x|$x->max()
    ),
    'DerivAffirmMaxVersion'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    'DerivAffirmTimestampDate'->func(
      x|$x->min()
    ),
    'DerivAffirmCreationDate'
  )->filter(
    row|((($row.getInteger('DerivAffirmVersion') ==
      $row.getNumber('DerivAffirmMaxVersion')) &&
      ($row.getString('Status') == 'REQUIRED')) &&
      !$row.getString('ContractId')->contains('.')) &&
      ($row.getString('ConfirmPlatform') == 'MARKITWIRE')
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::tradeProcessing::dealEvent.all()->filter(
      x|$x.lakePartition >= 19723
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.dealId,
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.dealVersion,
        x|$x.affirmationAttributes.affirmationStatus->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.eventAttributes.traderBookingLocation->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.eventDate->toOne(),
        x|$x->HarmonizedMasterDataRequirements::sourcing::envelope::primaryAssetClass::primaryAssetClass()->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.secDbCalculatorName->toOne(),
        x|$x->HarmonizedMasterDataRequirements::sourcing::envelope::eventType::eventType()->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.deal.party1->subType(@model::producers::operations::contractFactory::latest2x::trading::contract::event::processing::AccountDealParty).account.identifier->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.deal.party2->subType(@model::producers::operations::contractFactory::latest2x::trading::contract::event::processing::AccountDealParty).account.identifier->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.deal.party2->subType(@model::producers::operations::contractFactory::latest2x::trading::contract::event::processing::GSOEDealParty).gsOE.identifier->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.eventAttributes.legacyFields.secDbEventType->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.eventAttributes.secDbFields.tradeType->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.action->toOne()->toString(),
        x|$x.eventAttributes.secDbFields.riskTrades.dealId
      ],
      [
        'DealEventDealId',
        'DealEventId',
        'Version',
        'DealVersion',
        'DealEventAffirmationStatus',
        'TraderBookingLocation',
        'EventDate',
        'PrimaryAssetClass',
        'Calculator',
        'EventTypeName',
        'party1Original',
        'party2Original',
        'party2OEOriginal',
        'SecDbEventType',
        'TradeType',
        'DealEventAction',
        'RiskTradesDealId'
      ]
    )->olapGroupBy(
      ['DealEventDealId'],
      'DealVersion'->func(
        x|$x->max()
      ),
      'DealMaxVersion'
    )->filter(
      row|(((($row.getNumber('DealMaxVersion') ==
        $row.getNumber('DealVersion')) &&
        (($row.getString('SecDbEventType') != 'Termination') &&
        ($row.getString('TradeType') != 'Termination'))) &&
        ($row.getString('DealEventAffirmationStatus') != 'CONFIRMED')) &&
        ($row.getEnum('DealEventAction')->toString() != 'Cancel')) &&
        ($row.getString('DealEventDealId') != $row.getNumber('RiskTradesDealId'))
    )->extend(
      [
        col(
          r: TDSRow[1]|if(
            $r.getString('party2OEOriginal')->splitPart(
              ':',
              1
            )->toOne()->trim()->matches('[0-9]+'),
            |$r.getString('party2OEOriginal')->splitPart(
              ':',
              1
            )->toOne()->cast(@Integer),
            |0
          ),
          'party2OESplit'
        ),
        col(
          r: TDSRow[1]|$r.getString('party1Original')->left(8),
          'party1'
        ),
        col(
          r: TDSRow[1]|$r.getString('party2Original')->left(9),
          'party2'
        )
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.INNER,
    ['ContractId'],
    ['DealEventDealId']
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|$r.getDateTime('DerivAffirmCreationDate')->dateDiff(
          $businessDate,
          meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.DAYS
        ),
        'DaysSinceConfirmCreation'
      )
    ]
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::valuation::bcxDealNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasure.all()->otcConsumerModel::function::valuation::bcxDealLatestNetMonetaryMeasure(
      $businessDate
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['RiskTradesDealId'],
    ['HoldableId']
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|$r.getDate('EventDate')->dateDiff(
          $businessDate,
          meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.DAYS
        ),
        'DaysSinceEventDate'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|'N/A',
        'ContractEventId'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|0,
        'ContractEventVersion'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|'N/A',
        'ContractEventStatus'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|'N/A',
        'Comments'
      )
    ]
  )->join(
    model::domain::referenceData::account::FirmAccount.all($businessDate)->project(
      [
        x|$x.accountNumber,
        x|$x.preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).incomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy.businessLevel3.name,
        x|$x.preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).incomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy.businessLevel6.name
      ],
      [
        'accountNumber',
        'SbhLevel3',
        'SbhLevel6'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['party1'],
    ['accountNumber']
  )->join(
    model::domain::referenceData::account::Account.all($businessDate)->project(
      [
        x|$x.accountNumber,
        x|$x.beneficialOwnerEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.investmentAdvisorEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.gsLegalEntity.gsCompanyAcronym,
        x|$x.organizationalEntity($businessDate, $businessDate).bookableEntity.reportingEntity.divisionalReportingGroup.name,
        x|$x.organizationalEntity($businessDate, $businessDate).bookableEntity.name
      ],
      [
        'accountNumber',
        'BeneficialOwnerLegalName',
        'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'GsCompany',
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_Account',
        'FacetBookableEntityName_Account'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['party2'],
    ['accountNumber']
  )->join(
    model::domain::referenceData::entity::secdivClient::v2::BookableEntity.all($businessDate, $businessDate)->filter(
      x|($x.entityType == 'OE') &&
        !$x.organizationalEntity.aliasNumber->isEmpty()
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.organizationalEntity.aliasNumber,
        x|$x.name,
        x|$x.reportingEntity.divisionalReportingGroup.name
      ],
      [
        'OrganizationalEntityAliasNumber',
        'FacetBookableEntityName_OE',
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_OE'
      ]
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['party2OESplit'],
    ['OrganizationalEntityAliasNumber']
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          ($r.getString('FacetBookableEntityName_Account') != '') &&
            !$r.getString('FacetBookableEntityName_Account')->isEmpty(),
          |$r.getString('FacetBookableEntityName_Account'),
          |$r.getString('FacetBookableEntityName_OE')
        ),
        'FacetBookableEntityName'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          ($r.getString('FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_Account') != '') &&
            !$r.getString('FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_Account')->isEmpty(),
          |$r.getString('FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_Account'),
          |$r.getString('FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName_OE')
        ),
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName'
      )
    ]
  )->restrict(
    [
      'ContractEventId',
      'ContractEventVersion',
      'TraderBookingLocation',
      'EventDate',
      'SbhLevel3',
      'SbhLevel6',
      'BeneficialOwnerLegalName',
      'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
      'GsCompany',
      'FacetBookableEntityName',
      'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
      'PrimaryAssetClass',
      'Calculator',
      'EventTypeName',
      'ContractEventStatus',
      'ContractId',
      'DaysSinceEventDate',
      'DaysSinceConfirmCreation',
      'ConfirmId',
      'ConfirmPlatform',
      'RenderingChannel',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'Status',
      'Reason',
      'Comments',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'ValuationType',
      'Currency',
      'GroupType',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )
}

function {meta::pure::profiles::doc.doc = 'Pull confirm platform and rendering channel from related LEGAL confirms to enrich FINANCIAL confirms with missing values'} otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unaffirmedFinancialConfirms::getMissingUnaffirmedPlatforms(refinedDerivativeConfirms: otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedDerivativeConfirms->filter(
    x|((($x.affirmationType->isEmpty() &&
      (($x.confirmType == 'IncomingConfirm') &&
      ((($x.confirmRole == 'LEGAL') &&
      ($x.source != 'CCT')) &&
      ($x.sourceSystem != 'CCT')))) &&
      !($x.renderingChannel->isEmpty() &&
      $x.confirmPlatform->isEmpty())) &&
      $x.domain->in(
      [
        'SNOWDON',
        'DOM',
        'KASAI',
        'CONGO',
        'ELBRUS',
        'UBANGI',
        'SANGHA',
        'NILE',
        'MCKINLEY',
        'GANGES',
        'INDUS',
        'SUTLEJ',
        'RHINE',
        'VOLGA',
        'SANFORD',
        'YANGTZE',
        'DANUBE'
      ]
    )) &&
      ($x.timeUpdated->datePart() <=
      $businessDate)
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.objectId,
      x|$x.contractEventId,
      x|$x.version,
      x|$x.techVersion,
      x|$x.timeUpdated,
      x|$x.confirmPlatform,
      x|$x.renderingChannel
    ],
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventId',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'ConfirmTechVersion',
      'TimeUpdated',
      'RelatedLegalConfirmPlatform',
      'RelatedLegalConfirmRenderingChannel'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'ConfirmId',
      'ConfirmVersion',
      'TimeUpdated'
    ],
    desc('ConfirmTechVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'techVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('techVersionIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    desc('TimeUpdated'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'timeUpdatedIndex'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ConfirmId'],
    desc('ConfirmVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'confirmVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|($row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('confirmVersionIndex') == 1)) ||
      (!$row.getDateTime('TimeUpdated')->isEmpty() &&
      ($row.getNumber('timeUpdatedIndex') == 1))
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventId'],
    desc('RelatedLegalConfirmPlatform'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventIdIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventIdIndex') == 1
  )->restrict(
    [
      'RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventId',
      'RelatedLegalConfirmPlatform',
      'RelatedLegalConfirmRenderingChannel'
    ]
  )
}

function {meta::pure::profiles::doc.doc = 'Extracts USD Reference Rates for each day with precedence logic added to only output a single record per currency, per day (e.g. if both FEDFUNDS and LIBOR reference rates exist, only FEDFUNDS will be taken)'} otcConsumerModel::function::referenceRate::getUsdReferenceRates(fxReferenceRates: otcConsumerModel::model::referenceRate::fxReferenceRateNonMilestoned[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $fxReferenceRates->filter(
    x|($x.observationDate <=
      $businessDate) &&
      (($x.settlementDate ==
      $x.observationDate) &&
      ($x.observationDate >
      $businessDate->meta::pure::functions::date::adjust(
      meta::pure::functions::math::minus(2),
      meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.YEARS
    )))
  )->project(
    [
      x|$x.currency,
      x|$x.observationDate,
      x|$x.observationLocation,
      x|$x.observationSource,
      x|$x.observationLocationRanking,
      x|$x.observationSourceRanking,
      x|$x.rate
    ],
    [
      'Currency',
      'ObservationDate',
      'ObservationLocation',
      'ObservationSource',
      'ObservationLocationRanking',
      'ObservationSourceRanking',
      'UsdFxReferenceRate'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'Currency',
      'ObservationDate'
    ],
    asc('ObservationLocationRanking'),
    x|$x->denseRank(),
    'ObservationLocationRankIndex'
  )->olapGroupBy(
    [
      'Currency',
      'ObservationDate'
    ],
    asc('ObservationSourceRanking'),
    x|$x->denseRank(),
    'ObservationSourceRankIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|($row.getNumber('ObservationLocationRankIndex') == 1D) &&
      ($row.getNumber('ObservationSourceRankIndex') == 1D)
  )
}

function otcConsumerModel::function::valuation::bcxDealLatestNetMonetaryMeasure(bcxDealNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasures: otcConsumerModel::model::valuation::bcxDealNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasure[*], businessDate: StrictDate[1]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $bcxDealNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasures->filter(
    x|(($x.valuationDate >
      $businessDate->meta::pure::functions::date::adjust(
      meta::pure::functions::math::minus(2),
      meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.YEARS
    )) &&
      ($x.valuationDate <=
      $businessDate)) &&
      ($x.lake_out_id == 999999999)
  )->groupBy(
    [
      x|$x.holdableId,
      x|$x.valuationDate,
      x|$x.valuationScenario,
      x|$x.currency,
      x|$x.valuationDealScenarioRanking,
      x|'N/A',
      x|'N/A'
    ],
    [
      agg(
        x|$x.amount,
        x|$x->sum()->abs()
      )
    ],
    [
      'HoldableId',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'Currency',
      'ValuationScenarioRanking',
      'ValuationType',
      'GroupType',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    desc('ValuationDate'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxValuationDateIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxValuationDateIndex') == 1
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['HoldableId'],
    asc('ValuationScenarioRanking'),
    x|$x->rank(),
    'bcxValuationScenarioIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('bcxValuationScenarioIndex') == 1
  )->restrict(
    [
      'HoldableId',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'ValuationType',
      'Currency',
      'GroupType',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )
}

      'FinancialConfirmPlatform',
      'FinancialConfirmRenderingChannel',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'DerivConfirmCreationDate'
    ]
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|$r.getDateTime('DerivConfirmCreationDate')->dateDiff(
          $businessDate,
          meta::pure::functions::date::DurationUnit.DAYS
        ),
        'DaysSinceConfirmCreation'
      )
    ]
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm.all()->otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unaffirmedFinancialConfirms::getMissingUnaffirmedPlatforms(
      $businessDate
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['RelatedContractEventId'],
    ['RelatedLegalConfirmContractEventId']
  )->extend(
    [
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          $r.getString('FinancialConfirmPlatform')->isEmpty(),
          |$r.getString('RelatedLegalConfirmPlatform'),
          |$r.getString('FinancialConfirmPlatform')
        ),
        'ConfirmPlatform'
      ),
      col(
        r: TDSRow[1]|if(
          $r.getString('FinancialConfirmRenderingChannel')->isEmpty(),
          |$r.getString('RelatedLegalConfirmRenderingChannel'),
          |$r.getString('FinancialConfirmRenderingChannel')
        ),
        'RenderingChannel'
      )
    ]
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::tradeProcessing::refinedContractEvent.all()->filter(
      x|!(($x.secDbTradeableClassification == 'CT Funding Fixed') ||
        ($x.secDbTradeableClassification == 'CT Funding Float')) &&
        ($x.eventDate->datePart() <=
        $businessDate)
    )->project(
      [
        x|$x.objectId,
        x|$x.version,
        x|$x.traderBookingLocation,
        x|$x.eventDate,
        x|if(
        $x.riskAccountId->isEmpty(),
        |$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel3.name,
        |$x.riskAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel3.name
      ),
        x|if(
        $x.riskAccountId->isEmpty(),
        |$x.firmAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel6.name,
        |$x.riskAccountDetails($businessDate).preJvIncomeFunction($businessDate).standardBusinessHierarchy($businessDate).businessLevel6.name
      ),
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).beneficialOwnerEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).investmentAdvisorEntity.legalName,
        x|$x.accountDetails($businessDate).gsLegalEntity.gsCompanyAcronym,
        x|$x.facetClientDetails($businessDate, $businessDate).name,
        x|$x.facetClientDetails($businessDate, $businessDate).reportingEntity.divisionalReportingGroup.name,
        x|$x.primaryAssetClass,
        x|$x.secDbTradeableClassification,
        x|$x.tradeType,
        x|$x.contractEventStatus,
        x|$x.contractId,
        x|$x.age($businessDate)
      ],
      [
        'ContractEventId',
        'ContractEventVersion',
        'TraderBookingLocation',
        'EventDate',
        'SbhLevel3',
        'SbhLevel6',
        'BeneficialOwnerLegalName',
        'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
        'GsCompany',
        'FacetBookableEntityName',
        'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
        'PrimaryAssetClass',
        'Calculator',
        'EventTypeName',
        'ContractEventStatus',
        'ContractId',
        'DaysSinceEventDate'
      ]
    )->distinct(),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.INNER,
    [
      'RelatedContractEventId',
      'RelatedContractEventVersion'
    ],
    [
      'ContractEventId',
      'ContractEventVersion'
    ]
  )->olapGroupBy(
    ['ContractEventId'],
    desc('ContractEventVersion'),
    x|$x->rowNumber(),
    'contractEventVersionIndex'
  )->filter(
    row|$row.getNumber('contractEventVersionIndex') == 1
  )->join(
    otcConsumerModel::model::valuation::bcxNonMilestonedMonetaryMeasure.all()->otcConsumerModel::function::valuation::bcxLatestNetMonetaryMeasure(
      $businessDate
    ),
    meta::relational::metamodel::join::JoinType.LEFT_OUTER,
    ['ContractId'],
    ['HoldableId']
  )->restrict(
    [
      'ContractEventId',
      'ContractEventVersion',
      'TraderBookingLocation',
      'EventDate',
      'SbhLevel3',
      'SbhLevel6',
      'BeneficialOwnerLegalName',
      'InvestmentAdvisorLegalName',
      'GsCompany',
      'FacetBookableEntityName',
      'FacetDivisionalReportingGroupName',
      'PrimaryAssetClass',
      'Calculator',
      'EventTypeName',
      'ContractEventStatus',
      'ContractId',
      'DaysSinceEventDate',
      'DaysSinceConfirmCreation',
      'ConfirmId',
      'ConfirmPlatform',
      'RenderingChannel',
      'DerivConfirmAssetClass',
      'Status',
      'Reason',
      'Comments',
      'ValuationDate',
      'ValuationScenario',
      'ValuationType',
      'Currency',
      'GroupType',
      'BcxAbsoluteNetAmount'
    ]
  )->concatenate(
    otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::derivAffirm.all()->otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unaffirmedFinancialConfirms::directUnaffirmedFinancialConfirms(
      $businessDate
    )
  )
}

function {meta::pure::profiles::doc.doc = 'Identifies confirm population which are FX, ICON_VANILLA_TRADE priority reason code. Used to exclude records in downstream functions'} otcConsumerModel::function::confirm::unsignedLegalConfirms::refinedDerivativeConfirmFxVanillaTrade(refinedDerivativeConfirms: otcConsumerModel::model::confirm::refinedDerivativeConfirm[*]): meta::pure::tds::TabularDataSet[1]
{
  $refinedDerivativeConfirms->filter(
    x|((($x.confirmType == 'IncomingConfirm') &&
      ($x.priorityReason == 'ICON_VANILLA_TRADE')) &&
      ($x.derivConfirmAssetClass == 'FX')) &&
      ($x.confirmRole == 'LEGAL')
  )->groupBy(
    [
      x|$x.contractEventId,
      x|'YES'
    ],
    [
      agg(
        x|$x.contractEventId,
        x|$x->count()
      )
    ],
    [
      'RelatedContractEventId_FXVanillaTrade',
      'VanillaTrade',
      'count_vanillaTrade'
    ]
  )
}

###Connection
RelationalDatabaseConnection otcConsumerModel::connection::dmdaOtcConnectionFICCVW
{
  store: otcConsumerModel::store::otcConsumerStore;
  type: Snowflake;
  specification: Snowflake
  {
    name: 'DATALAKE_PROD_DB';
    account: 'sfgmdawseast1p01';
    warehouse: 'DMDA_CONSUMER_RO_WH';
    region: 'us-east-1';
    cloudType: 'aws';
    accountType: VPS;
    organization: 'goldman';
    role: 'PUBLIC';
  };
  auth: OAuth
  {
    oauthKey: 'idfs';
    scopeName: 'SESSION:ROLE-ANY';
  };
  postProcessors:
  [
    lakeMapper
    {
      mappers:
      [
        schema {from: 'AMHub'; to: 'AMHub_PC1_PROD';},
        schema {from: 'EMMA'; to: 'EMMA_PC1_PROD';},
        schema {from: 'tams'; to: 'TAMS_STORE';},
        schema {from: 'FACET_Client'; to: 'FACET_Client_PROD';},
        schema {from: 'GlobalMarketsDI'; to: 'CLIENT_LISTS';},
        schema {from: 'delp_prod_hcm_person_datastore_public'; to: 'HCM_PERSON_DATASTORE_PUBLIC';},
        schema {from: 'Prime'; to: 'Prime_PROD';},
        schema {from: 'Choice_SPA'; to: 'CHOICE_PROD';},
        table {from: 'SPA_source'; to: 'SPA'; schemaFrom: 'Choice_SPA'; schemaTo: 'CHOICE_PROD';}
      ];
    },
    lake
    {
      warehouse: 'FDE_SF_VW';
      mode: Prod;
      lakeTableTypes: LakeOnly;
      secureViewManagement: Active;
      applyPostProcessorsToSecuredDatasets: true;
    }
  ];
}

RelationalDatabaseConnection otcConsumerModel::connection::dmdaOtcConnection
{
  store: otcConsumerModel::store::otcConsumerStore;
  type: Snowflake;
  specification: Snowflake
  {
    name: 'DATALAKE_PROD_DB';
    account: 'sfgmdawseast1p01';

    cloudType: 'aws';
    accountType: VPS;
    organization: 'goldman';
    role: 'PUBLIC';
  };

    scopeName: 'SESSION:ROLE-ANY';

  postProcessors:

    lake
    {
      warehouse: 'FDE_SF_VW';
      mode: Prod;
      lakeTableTypes: LakeOnly;
      secureViewManagement: Active;
      applyPostProcessorsToSecuredDatasets: true;
    }
  ];
}
